# Research Plan

Last updated: March 30, 2026

This file is the living research task board for the active manuscript line of `The Æther-Flow Interpretation of Relativity`.

## Purpose

Use this plan to track:

- tasks already completed
- tasks currently active
- tasks still to be done
- new tasks added as the research line evolves

## Update Rules

- mark completed tasks with `[x]`
- leave open tasks as `[ ]`
- add newly discovered work under `New Tasks To Triage` first
- once a new task is accepted as active work, move it into the appropriate section below
- when a task changes the research direction, add one short note to `Research Log`

## Current Objective

As of March 30, 2026, the active objective has changed. The repository is no longer in packaging-freeze mode. The overview-first exact-closure sequence remains the benchmark theory statement and must still be presented first: [aether_flow_exact_closure_sequence_overview.tex](manuscripts/active/tex/aether_flow_exact_closure_sequence_overview.tex), [aether_flow_exact_closure_note.tex](manuscripts/active/tex/aether_flow_exact_closure_note.tex), [aether_flow_foundations.tex](manuscripts/active/tex/aether_flow_foundations.tex), [aether_flow_dynamics.tex](manuscripts/active/tex/aether_flow_dynamics.tex), [aether_flow_consistency.tex](manuscripts/active/tex/aether_flow_consistency.tex), [aether_flow_relativistic_recovery.tex](manuscripts/active/tex/aether_flow_relativistic_recovery.tex), and [aether_flow_geometry.tex](manuscripts/active/tex/aether_flow_geometry.tex).

The research goal is now to derive GR from `The Æther-Flow Interpretation of Relativity` while keeping that benchmark fixed and the claim boundary honest. The immediate task is no longer another repository-facing cleanup pass, and it is no longer, by default, another still-deeper origin note on the anchored positive-pair side line. The benchmark-gates extraction is now recorded in [aether_flow_exact_closure_derivation_gates_note.tex](manuscripts/active/tex/aether_flow_exact_closure_derivation_gates_note.tex), the observer-side obstruction classification is now recorded in [aether_flow_substrate_higher_derivative_observer_remainder_classification_note.tex](manuscripts/active/tex/aether_flow_substrate_higher_derivative_observer_remainder_classification_note.tex), the benchmark-facing redesign screen is now recorded in [aether_flow_substrate_higher_derivative_substrate_response_self_response_bridge_redesign_gate_screen_note.tex](manuscripts/active/tex/aether_flow_substrate_higher_derivative_substrate_response_self_response_bridge_redesign_gate_screen_note.tex), and the one-metric charge-polarization sequence is now recorded through [aether_flow_substrate_response_charge_polarization_exact_preservation_primitive_substrate_root_generating_shell_lifted_connection_cotangent_parallel_transport_origin_note.tex](manuscripts/active/tex/aether_flow_substrate_response_charge_polarization_exact_preservation_primitive_substrate_root_generating_shell_lifted_connection_cotangent_parallel_transport_origin_note.tex).

At disciplined primitive-substrate / root-generating shell / lifted connection-cotangent / parallel-transport scope, that newest note shows that the previous primitive layer is itself the shell-restricted image of a still deeper subprimitive layer: the recorded primitive substrate bundles arise as zero shells of subprimitive substrate bundles, the recorded root-generating shell sections arise from lifted root-generating shell maps, the recorded lifted pre-ambient-generating shell maps arise from deeper lifted pre-ambient-generating shell maps, the recorded lifted ambient-generating shell maps arise from deeper lifted ambient-generating shell maps, the recorded lifted shell maps and lifted exact-constraint maps with the same target metrics arise from deeper lifted shell and exact-constraint maps, the recorded primitive cotangent-model Liouville one-form / closed two-form geometry arises from subprimitive cotangent-model Liouville data, the recorded primitive connection one-forms and induced parallel transports arise from subprimitive connection one-forms and their induced parallel transports, and the recorded primitive-basic shadow / rate / density / flux / boundary data together with the same fixed-endpoint primitive rate-action geometry arise from subprimitive-basic and subprimitive-action geometry. The same primitive layer, the same root-shell / lifted connection-cotangent / parallel-transport layer, the same pre-ambient-shell / connection-cotangent / parallel-transport layer, the same ambient-shell / cotangent-Liouville / connection-holonomy layer, the same process-state layer, and the same reversible process-thread / process-window / history / groupoid / reconfiguration / derivation downstream chain are therefore recovered again, and with them the same \(\StemFunctional\), the same exact-preservation normal form, the same carrier-origin functional, the same primitive reservoir, the same microscopic-equilibrium completion reservoir, the same \(\Sigma^{\mathrm{cmp}}\) solve, the same \(\Pi_{\mathrm{free}}H=0\) outcome, the same observer-equation closure, the same one-operative-metric route, and the same recorded Phase D / E and Phase F gains. The immediate primary task is now to derive or justify a still-deeper origin or sharper selection principle below that newer subprimitive construction itself, explaining why the subprimitive substrate bundles, primitive-generating shell sections, lifted root-generating shell maps, lifted pre-ambient-generating shell maps, lifted ambient-generating shell maps, lifted shell maps and lifted exact-constraint maps with the same target metrics, subprimitive cotangent-model Liouville one-forms and closed two-form geometry, subprimitive connection one-forms and their induced parallel transports, subprimitive-basic shadow / rate / density / flux / boundary data, and fixed-endpoint subprimitive rate-action geometry are forced by yet more primitive substrate structure while re-showing the same primitive substrate / root-generating shell / lifted connection-cotangent layer, the same root-shell / lifted connection-cotangent / parallel-transport layer, the same pre-ambient-shell / connection-cotangent / parallel-transport layer, the same ambient-shell / cotangent-Liouville / connection-holonomy layer, the same process-state layer, the same reversible process-thread / process-window / history / groupoid / reconfiguration downstream chain, the same \(\StemFunctional\), the same exact-preservation normal form, the same carrier-origin functional, the same primitive reservoir, the same microscopic-equilibrium completion reservoir, the same \(\Sigma^{\mathrm{cmp}}\) solve, the same \(\Pi_{\mathrm{free}}H=0\) outcome, the same observer-equation closure, and the preserved one-operative-metric, Phase D / E, and Phase F package, or else to produce another comparably concrete observer-equation gain on the same one-metric charge-polarization line. Only after that deeper burden is met should any stronger promotion language be revisited. The anchored positive-pair side line remains non-primary unless it supplies that deeper burden or another concrete observer-equation gain.

The raw-vacuum-orbit-origin note now exists as [aether_flow_substrate_higher_derivative_nonlocal_bridge_self_response_off_shell_profile_selection_bridge_order_raw_vacuum_orbit_origin_note.tex](manuscripts/active/tex/aether_flow_substrate_higher_derivative_nonlocal_bridge_self_response_off_shell_profile_selection_bridge_order_raw_vacuum_orbit_origin_note.tex). It records that the raw positive vacuum orbit itself is generated as the minimizing family of a deeper primitive orbit-modulus sector while preserving the same recovered density/current block, the same composite primitive bridge-order block, the same phase-neutral minimizing branch, the same canonical profile, and the same downstream dressed bridge package. The deeper verdict is disciplined rather than negative: the positive scale orbit is now derived, but not yet quotiented, so canonical normalization remains the honest representative choice rather than a proved deeper redundancy, and the surviving global \(O(2)\) vacuum angle remains residual because this deeper layer adds neither locking nor quotient structure.

The orbit-shape/modulus burden-fixing note now exists as [aether_flow_substrate_higher_derivative_nonlocal_bridge_self_response_off_shell_profile_selection_bridge_order_orbit_shape_modulus_origin_note.tex](manuscripts/active/tex/aether_flow_substrate_higher_derivative_nonlocal_bridge_self_response_off_shell_profile_selection_bridge_order_orbit_shape_modulus_origin_note.tex). That note fixes the active burden below the raw-vacuum-orbit layer: any still-deeper continuation must derive or sharply constrain the unit-reference orbit-shape block and the unanchored positive orbit modulus from still more primitive substrate structure, prove that the same recovered density/current block, the same composite primitive bridge-order block, the same phase-neutral minimizing branch, the same canonical profile, and the same downstream dressed bridge package are recovered unchanged, and revisit the scale-orbit and residual vacuum-angle verdicts only if the deeper layer naturally supplies genuine quotient or locking structure.

That direct continuation was not yet cleanly formulable at the next step, so the narrow setup note [aether_flow_substrate_higher_derivative_nonlocal_bridge_self_response_off_shell_profile_selection_bridge_order_orbit_shape_modulus_primitive_class_setup_note.tex](manuscripts/active/tex/aether_flow_substrate_higher_derivative_nonlocal_bridge_self_response_off_shell_profile_selection_bridge_order_orbit_shape_modulus_primitive_class_setup_note.tex) was written immediately below it. That note fixes the minimal primitive variable class and the factorization from that class into the unit-reference orbit-shape block and positive orbit modulus, proves that the same recovered density/current block, the same composite primitive bridge-order block, the same phase-neutral minimizing branch, the same canonical profile, and the same downstream dressed bridge package must remain fixed, and leaves the scale-orbit and residual vacuum-angle verdicts unchanged unless genuine quotient or locking structure later appears.

That first direct continuation now exists as [aether_flow_substrate_higher_derivative_nonlocal_bridge_self_response_off_shell_profile_selection_bridge_order_orbit_shape_modulus_primitive_class_amplitude_lift_origin_note.tex](manuscripts/active/tex/aether_flow_substrate_higher_derivative_nonlocal_bridge_self_response_off_shell_profile_selection_bridge_order_orbit_shape_modulus_primitive_class_amplitude_lift_origin_note.tex). It chooses the first concrete deeper sector below the setup interface, realizes the primitive class as the finite sign quotient of a signed amplitude sector, reproduces the same raw-orbit lift and same downstream dressed bridge package, and keeps the scale-orbit and residual vacuum-angle verdicts unchanged because the new quotient is internal only to square-root representatives.

That next deeper layer now also exists as [aether_flow_substrate_higher_derivative_nonlocal_bridge_self_response_off_shell_profile_selection_bridge_order_orbit_shape_modulus_primitive_class_amplitude_sector_origin_note.tex](manuscripts/active/tex/aether_flow_substrate_higher_derivative_nonlocal_bridge_self_response_off_shell_profile_selection_bridge_order_orbit_shape_modulus_primitive_class_amplitude_sector_origin_note.tex). It realizes the signed amplitude sector itself as the image of a deeper oriented absolute-amplitude sector, traces the old finite sign quotient to polarity forgetting, reproduces the same raw-orbit lift and same downstream dressed bridge package, and keeps the scale-orbit and residual vacuum-angle verdicts unchanged because the only quotient is still internal to the amplitude representatives.

That next deeper layer now also exists as [aether_flow_substrate_higher_derivative_nonlocal_bridge_self_response_off_shell_profile_selection_bridge_order_orbit_shape_modulus_primitive_class_absolute_amplitude_polarity_origin_note.tex](manuscripts/active/tex/aether_flow_substrate_higher_derivative_nonlocal_bridge_self_response_off_shell_profile_selection_bridge_order_orbit_shape_modulus_primitive_class_absolute_amplitude_polarity_origin_note.tex). It realizes the positive absolute-amplitude block and discrete polarity data as the image of a deeper unequal positive-pair sector, traces those oriented data to gap magnitudes and order signs of unequal positive pairs, reproduces the same raw-orbit lift and same downstream dressed bridge package, and keeps the scale-orbit and residual vacuum-angle verdicts unchanged because the only new quotient is the internal pair-fiber quotient.

That next deeper layer now also exists as [aether_flow_substrate_higher_derivative_nonlocal_bridge_self_response_off_shell_profile_selection_bridge_order_orbit_shape_modulus_primitive_class_absolute_amplitude_polarity_midpoint_fiber_origin_note.tex](manuscripts/active/tex/aether_flow_substrate_higher_derivative_nonlocal_bridge_self_response_off_shell_profile_selection_bridge_order_orbit_shape_modulus_primitive_class_absolute_amplitude_polarity_midpoint_fiber_origin_note.tex). It realizes the unequal positive-pair sector itself as the image of a deeper midpoint/fiber sector, makes the pair layer canonically equivalent to positive midpoint and signed fiber-fraction data, shows that once an oriented absolute-amplitude datum and midpoint tuple are fixed the signed fiber fractions are uniquely forced, reproduces the same raw-orbit lift and same downstream dressed bridge package, and keeps the scale-orbit and residual vacuum-angle verdicts unchanged because the only new relation is the internal midpoint/fiber relation rather than a genuine positive-modulus or angle quotient.

That next deeper layer now also exists as [aether_flow_substrate_higher_derivative_nonlocal_bridge_self_response_off_shell_profile_selection_bridge_order_orbit_shape_modulus_primitive_class_absolute_amplitude_polarity_midpoint_selection_note.tex](manuscripts/active/tex/aether_flow_substrate_higher_derivative_nonlocal_bridge_self_response_off_shell_profile_selection_bridge_order_orbit_shape_modulus_primitive_class_absolute_amplitude_polarity_midpoint_selection_note.tex). It rewrites the residual midpoint freedom as a selector fiber over the oriented absolute-amplitude layer, defines the induced map into the midpoint/fiber and positive-pair layers, selects the balanced canonical midpoint representative \(C=\Abs\) with \(\Theta=\epsilon/2\), reproduces the same raw-orbit lift and same downstream dressed bridge package, and keeps the scale-orbit and residual vacuum-angle verdicts unchanged because the new structure is a canonical section rather than a genuine positive-modulus quotient or angle-locking mechanism.

That next deeper layer now also exists as [aether_flow_substrate_higher_derivative_nonlocal_bridge_self_response_off_shell_profile_selection_bridge_order_orbit_shape_modulus_primitive_class_absolute_amplitude_polarity_midpoint_selector_justification_note.tex](manuscripts/active/tex/aether_flow_substrate_higher_derivative_nonlocal_bridge_self_response_off_shell_profile_selection_bridge_order_orbit_shape_modulus_primitive_class_absolute_amplitude_polarity_midpoint_selector_justification_note.tex). It realizes the balanced midpoint selector itself as the unique equilibrium of a deeper normalized pair-balance sector, defines the induced map into the selector layer and hence through the midpoint/fiber, positive-pair, and oriented absolute-amplitude/polarity layers, reproduces the same signed amplitudes, primitive class, raw-orbit lift, phase-neutral minimizing branch, canonical profile, and downstream dressed bridge package, and keeps the scale-orbit and residual vacuum-angle verdicts unchanged because the new structure is still a positive-definite selection principle rather than a genuine positive-modulus quotient or angle-locking mechanism.

That next deeper layer now also exists as [aether_flow_substrate_higher_derivative_nonlocal_bridge_self_response_off_shell_profile_selection_bridge_order_orbit_shape_modulus_primitive_class_absolute_amplitude_polarity_midpoint_selector_pair_balance_origin_note.tex](manuscripts/active/tex/aether_flow_substrate_higher_derivative_nonlocal_bridge_self_response_off_shell_profile_selection_bridge_order_orbit_shape_modulus_primitive_class_absolute_amplitude_polarity_midpoint_selector_pair_balance_origin_note.tex). It realizes the normalized pair-balance sector itself as the projective image of a deeper anchored positive-pair sector, derives the current unit-balance energy as the reduced anchor-relative drift energy of that deeper sector, defines the induced map into the normalized pair-balance layer and hence through the selector, midpoint/fiber, positive-pair, and oriented absolute-amplitude/polarity layers, reproduces the same signed amplitudes, primitive class, raw-orbit lift, phase-neutral minimizing branch, canonical profile, and downstream dressed bridge package, and keeps the scale-orbit and residual vacuum-angle verdicts unchanged because the new quotient is internal only to the anchored normalization data rather than acting on the orbit scale or the vacuum angle.

The current honest next manuscript target on that deeper-origin side line is therefore a deeper origin or anchoring note for that anchored positive-pair sector itself below the midpoint-selector pair-balance-origin layer, revisiting the scale-orbit or residual vacuum-angle verdicts only if a still deeper structure actually supplies a quotient acting on the orbit scale or a genuine locking mechanism for the residual vacuum angle.

### Strategic Research Plan For The GR-Derivation Goal

The anchored positive-pair continuation above remains the honest next manuscript on the current deeper-origin side line. But the repository is now being judged by a stricter question than whether another disciplined origin note can be written. The real question is whether the active line is converging on a genuine derivation of GR rather than indefinitely extending internal structure below a still-fixed observer package.

The plan below therefore supplements the immediate side-line queue and fixes the primary derivation-critical agenda that should control manuscript priority from this point.

- The overview-first exact-closure package remains the fixed benchmark and public front door.
- The deeper selector / orbit-shape / anchored positive-pair line remains acceptable as a side continuation, but it no longer counts as primary evidence of progress toward GR derivation unless it supplies the deeper burden now missing below the exact-preservation charge-generator / continuity-Hessian origin note or another concrete observer-equation gain.
- Primary progress toward the project goal now means progress on at least one of the following fixed burdens:
  the exact Einstein observer equation or an equivalent Einstein--Hilbert plus ordinary matter action must be recovered from substrate variables;
  the single operative metric and universal matter coupling must survive without an unsuppressed preferred-frame matter term;
  the low-energy observer sector must retain the ordinary diffeomorphism/two-tensor content with no unsuppressed extra scalar/vector/ghost remainder;
  GR must arise as a controlled limit rather than as a hand-set cancellation locus;
  every leftover sector must be classified as gauge, constraint, heavy/decoupled, or a genuine testable deviation.

#### Phase A: Benchmark Extraction and Theorem Target

- [x] Write one short benchmark-facing note that extracts, from the overview and six core exact-closure manuscripts, the precise derivation target: Einstein equations or equivalent Einstein--Hilbert action, single-metric matter coupling, ordinary diffeomorphism/two-tensor content, exact causal/proper-time/null recovery, and zero genuine observer remainder.
  Completed in [aether_flow_exact_closure_derivation_gates_note.tex](manuscripts/active/tex/aether_flow_exact_closure_derivation_gates_note.tex).
- [x] Restate the exact-closure test from [aether_flow_substrate_kinematics.tex](manuscripts/active/tex/aether_flow_substrate_kinematics.tex) as a theorem target rather than only as a candidate-model checklist.
  Completed in [aether_flow_exact_closure_derivation_gates_note.tex](manuscripts/active/tex/aether_flow_exact_closure_derivation_gates_note.tex).
- [ ] Mark explicitly which existing downstream notes are interpretive/deeper-structure notes and which ones bear directly on the derivational theorem target.

#### Phase B: Observer-Remainder Obstruction Classification

- [x] Write a dedicated note classifying the currently surviving observer-side remainder tensor into longitudinal, off-longitudinal, gauge/constraint-exact, and genuinely physical pieces on the active nondegenerate branch.
  Completed in [aether_flow_substrate_higher_derivative_observer_remainder_classification_note.tex](manuscripts/active/tex/aether_flow_substrate_higher_derivative_observer_remainder_classification_note.tex).
- [x] Prove which parts of that remainder are unavoidable if the present bridge metric and present single-metric matter route are both kept fixed.
  Completed at current disciplined scope in [aether_flow_substrate_higher_derivative_observer_remainder_classification_note.tex](manuscripts/active/tex/aether_flow_substrate_higher_derivative_observer_remainder_classification_note.tex), which records why bridge-metric-only and matter-route-only repairs fail on matter-free reduced data.
- [x] Use that classification to decide whether the next admissible primary move is a bridge-metric redesign, an operational observer-map redesign, a matter-route redesign, or a deeper substrate response sector that changes the observer equation already on matter-free reduced data.
  Completed in [aether_flow_substrate_higher_derivative_observer_remainder_classification_note.tex](manuscripts/active/tex/aether_flow_substrate_higher_derivative_observer_remainder_classification_note.tex), which selects the deeper substrate-response / self-response bridge-redesign level as the next primary move.

#### Phase C: Bridge-Level Redesign Search

- [x] Restrict the next primary candidate search to bridge-level redesigns that can act on matter-free reduced data and can in principle cancel the recorded observer remainder without annihilating the ordered-flow equation.
  Completed in [aether_flow_substrate_higher_derivative_substrate_response_self_response_bridge_redesign_gate_screen_note.tex](manuscripts/active/tex/aether_flow_substrate_higher_derivative_substrate_response_self_response_bridge_redesign_gate_screen_note.tex), which records matter-free reduced activity and ordered-flow preservation as non-negotiable admissibility requirements.
- [x] Prioritize three candidate families first: modified bridge-metric functionals, modified operational observer maps, and deeper substrate response sectors whose elimination changes the observer equation nontrivially already in vacuum.
  Completed in [aether_flow_substrate_higher_derivative_substrate_response_self_response_bridge_redesign_gate_screen_note.tex](manuscripts/active/tex/aether_flow_substrate_higher_derivative_substrate_response_self_response_bridge_redesign_gate_screen_note.tex), which screens those families at benchmark-facing scope and selects the substrate-response / self-response family as the only live primary family.
- [x] For each candidate family, write the smallest admissibility note before theorem work begins: exact-closure answerability, single-metric matter route if retained, nondegenerate flat-background branch, and no by-construction Einsteinian closure.
  Completed at benchmark-facing screening scope in [aether_flow_substrate_higher_derivative_substrate_response_self_response_bridge_redesign_gate_screen_note.tex](manuscripts/active/tex/aether_flow_substrate_higher_derivative_substrate_response_self_response_bridge_redesign_gate_screen_note.tex), which records the admissibility package and immediate derivation-gate screen for the surviving primary family before theorem work.
- [x] Write the first explicit substrate-response / self-response candidate note inside the surviving primary family, specifying its response sector, operative observer metric, and self-response-neutral target, and derive the eliminated observer equation already on matter-free reduced data before any infrared or theorem claim is made.
  Completed in [aether_flow_substrate_higher_derivative_substrate_response_self_response_charge_polarization_candidate_note.tex](manuscripts/active/tex/aether_flow_substrate_higher_derivative_substrate_response_self_response_charge_polarization_candidate_note.tex), which records a slice-wise nonpropagating charge-potential plus constrained-polarization sector, derives the eliminated observer equation already on matter-free reduced data, preserves one operative metric with universal matter coupling, and gives a first infrared screen while leaving the full Phase D, E, F, and G verdicts open.

#### Phase D: Infrared Gauge and Spectrum Gate

- [x] For the recorded charge-polarization candidate, linearize the full coupled reduced system about an admissible homogeneous background and derive the low-energy observer-accessible spectrum explicitly.
  Completed in [aether_flow_substrate_higher_derivative_substrate_response_self_response_charge_polarization_infrared_spectrum_universal_coupling_gate_note.tex](manuscripts/active/tex/aether_flow_substrate_higher_derivative_substrate_response_self_response_charge_polarization_infrared_spectrum_universal_coupling_gate_note.tex), which derives the full coupled reduced linearization and its explicit infrared block structure on an admissible homogeneous benchmark branch.
- [x] Require ordinary diffeomorphism-compatible two-tensor propagation in the observer sector, or else prove that any extra scalar/vector sector is pure gauge, auxiliary, or parametrically decoupled.
  Completed at present benchmark-branch scope in [aether_flow_substrate_higher_derivative_substrate_response_self_response_charge_polarization_infrared_spectrum_universal_coupling_gate_note.tex](manuscripts/active/tex/aether_flow_substrate_higher_derivative_substrate_response_self_response_charge_polarization_infrared_spectrum_universal_coupling_gate_note.tex), which shows that only the ordinary GR two-tensor sector propagates unsuppressed while the charge-polarization response fields remain elliptic or algebraic.
- [x] Reject any branch with an unsuppressed preferred-frame matter signature, second low-energy causal cone, ghost, or tachyon.
  Completed at present benchmark-branch scope in [aether_flow_substrate_higher_derivative_substrate_response_self_response_charge_polarization_infrared_spectrum_universal_coupling_gate_note.tex](manuscripts/active/tex/aether_flow_substrate_higher_derivative_substrate_response_self_response_charge_polarization_infrared_spectrum_universal_coupling_gate_note.tex), which records the no-unsuppressed preferred-frame / second-cone / ghost / tachyon verdict for the concrete candidate at linear infrared order.

#### Phase E: Universal Matter-Coupling Gate

- [x] Prove that matter and light continue to couple through one operative metric in the observer-accessible regime.
  Completed in [aether_flow_substrate_higher_derivative_substrate_response_self_response_charge_polarization_infrared_spectrum_universal_coupling_gate_note.tex](manuscripts/active/tex/aether_flow_substrate_higher_derivative_substrate_response_self_response_charge_polarization_infrared_spectrum_universal_coupling_gate_note.tex), which re-derives the eliminated matter and light sector and shows that all observer-side coupling still runs through the single operative metric \(\CandidateMetric\).
- [x] If the matter route is modified, show that the resulting law is still equivalent to universal minimal coupling at exact-closure scope, or else record the branch honestly as outside exact closure.
  Completed at present eliminated-candidate scope in [aether_flow_substrate_higher_derivative_substrate_response_self_response_charge_polarization_infrared_spectrum_universal_coupling_gate_note.tex](manuscripts/active/tex/aether_flow_substrate_higher_derivative_substrate_response_self_response_charge_polarization_infrared_spectrum_universal_coupling_gate_note.tex), which shows that elimination changes the gravitational functional but introduces no new matter argument beyond \(\CandidateMetric\).
- [x] Check geodesic, null-cone, redshift, and proper-time recovery immediately after elimination, not only later in package-facing summaries.
  Completed in [aether_flow_substrate_higher_derivative_substrate_response_self_response_charge_polarization_infrared_spectrum_universal_coupling_gate_note.tex](manuscripts/active/tex/aether_flow_substrate_higher_derivative_substrate_response_self_response_charge_polarization_infrared_spectrum_universal_coupling_gate_note.tex), which records those recoveries directly after elimination rather than deferring them to later summaries.

#### Phase F: Controlled GR-Limit Theorem

- [x] For the first candidate that survives the previous gates, derive the observer equation in a controlled infrared limit with explicit scaling, regularity, and elimination assumptions.
  Completed in [aether_flow_substrate_higher_derivative_substrate_response_self_response_charge_polarization_controlled_gr_limit_note.tex](manuscripts/active/tex/aether_flow_substrate_higher_derivative_substrate_response_self_response_charge_polarization_controlled_gr_limit_note.tex), which fixes the admissible small-data decoupling regime, records the regularity and elimination hypotheses explicitly, and proves an observer-equation GR limit with quartic-order remainder control.
- [x] Show that the Einstein tensor and ordinary matter stress tensor emerge without choosing coefficients solely to force cancellation on a degenerate or tuned-by-construction branch.
  Completed in [aether_flow_substrate_higher_derivative_substrate_response_self_response_charge_polarization_controlled_gr_limit_note.tex](manuscripts/active/tex/aether_flow_substrate_higher_derivative_substrate_response_self_response_charge_polarization_controlled_gr_limit_note.tex), which derives the limit from scale separation, elliptic elimination, and one-metric matter coupling rather than from hand-set finite-amplitude cancellation.
- [x] State exactly which assumptions are dynamical, asymptotic, symmetry-based, constitutive, or still provisional.
  Completed in [aether_flow_substrate_higher_derivative_substrate_response_self_response_charge_polarization_controlled_gr_limit_note.tex](manuscripts/active/tex/aether_flow_substrate_higher_derivative_substrate_response_self_response_charge_polarization_controlled_gr_limit_note.tex), whose assumption ledger separates those five input classes explicitly.

#### Phase G: Residual-Sector Verdict

- [x] Classify every remaining substrate sector as gauge, constraint-exact, heavy/decoupled, or a genuine deviation sector.
  Completed in [aether_flow_substrate_higher_derivative_substrate_response_self_response_charge_polarization_residual_sector_verdict_note.tex](manuscripts/active/tex/aether_flow_substrate_higher_derivative_substrate_response_self_response_charge_polarization_residual_sector_verdict_note.tex), which decomposes the exact finite-\(\varepsilon\) remainder away from the decisive exterior cancellation regime, classifies all noncore sectors as absent, gauge exact, constraint exact, or decoupled, and isolates only the composite quartic tensor as still live.
- [x] If any deviation sector survives, derive its first observer-accessible consequences and compare them against the fixed exact-closure claim boundary before any promotion language is used.
  Completed in [aether_flow_substrate_higher_derivative_substrate_response_self_response_charge_polarization_residual_sector_verdict_note.tex](manuscripts/active/tex/aether_flow_substrate_higher_derivative_substrate_response_self_response_charge_polarization_residual_sector_verdict_note.tex), which records the first observer-accessible consequence only as a quartic-order correction tensor in the finite-\(\varepsilon\) observer equation and uses that to state the negative claim-boundary verdict at current scope.
- [x] Only after this step should a branch be described as a candidate deeper theory with GR as an emergent low-energy limit.
  Completed as a negative promotion verdict in [aether_flow_substrate_higher_derivative_substrate_response_self_response_charge_polarization_residual_sector_verdict_note.tex](manuscripts/active/tex/aether_flow_substrate_higher_derivative_substrate_response_self_response_charge_polarization_residual_sector_verdict_note.tex), which records that the present charge-polarization candidate is not yet fully closed and therefore is not yet promotable as a deeper theory with GR merely as its low-energy limit.

#### Near-Term Queue

- [x] Write a short bridge-program note that translates the benchmark package into five non-negotiable derivation gates and states explicitly that deeper selector/origin notes are secondary unless they discharge one of those gates.

### Current Public-Release Objective

The public-release objective is now secondary to the derivational program. The repository should still be deployable as an accessible GitHub project, but that work no longer substitutes for manuscript progress on the GR-derivation line. Deployment work should be treated as an ongoing maintenance layer beneath the resumed derivational line.

The immediate release-side maintenance tasks are:

- keep the GitHub Pages structure under `docs/` stable
- keep the front-facing article, reviewer guidance, and AI-collaboration note aligned with the benchmark-first claim boundary
- keep the curated PDF and LaTeX asset bundle answerable to the benchmark package
- surface the live derivational target only after the flagship package has been presented first

## Secondary Public Deployment Tasks

- [x] Create the first public-facing pages for `Home`, `Start Here`, `Theory Package`, `Research Archive`, `AI Collaboration and Method`, and `How To Review`.

- [x] Choose the first curated set of public PDFs and `.tex` files for release.
- [x] Simplify the root [README.md](README.md) as a GitHub landing page while preserving the existing claim boundary.

Those baseline deployment tasks are complete. The remaining release-side burden is maintenance: keep the benchmark package first, keep the claim boundary explicit, and surface the resumed derivational target only downstream of that benchmark.

## Active Research Program: New Candidate Branch

### Phase 1: Branch Design Criteria

- [x] Write the admissibility criteria for any new candidate branch.
  Criteria should include:
  exact-closure answerability, single-metric matter coupling, no unsuppressed preferred-frame matter term, and a health standard at least as strong as the current stable-sign branch.
- [x] List the smallest nonminimal modifications to the `S/Q/U` sector worth testing first.
  Candidate families may include:
  new derivative mixings, new constrained auxiliary structure, or higher-order operators that change the scalar cancellation problem without changing the public exact-closure claim.
- [x] Choose the first candidate branch to test and record why it is the preferred first branch.
  Completed: the derivative-mixing `S/Q` branch was selected as the first nonminimal branch worth testing.

### Phase 2: Candidate Branch Formulation

- [x] Write a dedicated manuscript for the new candidate branch.
- [x] State the modified action, all new symbols, and the intended exact-closure limit.
- [x] Record which parts of the minimal-action no-go are meant to be evaded and which benchmark requirements remain unchanged.
  Completed.

### Phase 3: Flat-Background Quadratic Test

- [x] Linearize the new branch about an admissible homogeneous bridge background.
- [x] Derive the new quadratic auxiliary coefficients explicitly.
- [x] Identify the replacement for the minimal-action scalar obstruction, whether it remains `\mathcal B(k^2)` or becomes a generalized operator.
- [x] Determine whether the new branch admits a nondegenerate flat-background exact-closure solution.
- [x] Check that no unsuppressed extra scalar, vector, or tensor pole survives in the observer-accessible infrared theory.
  Completed.
  Outcome:
  the derivative-mixing branch does not admit a nondegenerate flat-background exact-closure branch; exact closure survives only on a tuned semidefinite perfect-square branch.
